ConfidenceLevel.MEDIUM\n\n\nclass IntentClassifier:\n    """Classifies user input into intent categories"""\n    \n    # Intent patterns for rule-based classification\n    INTENT_PATTERNS = {\n        IntentCategory.QUERY: [\n            r\'\\b(what|who|where|when|why|how|show|list|get|find|search)\\b\',\n            r\'\\b(status|info|information|details|about)\\b\',\n        ],\n        IntentCategory.ACTION: [\n            r\'\\b(create|make|build|generate|start|run|execute|do)\\b\',\n            r\'\\b(initialize|setup|configure|deploy|launch)\\b\',\n        ],\n        IntentCategory.GUIDANCE: [\n            r\'\\b(help|guide|assist|recommend|suggest|advise)\\b\',\n            r\'\\b(should|could|would|best way|how to)\\b\',\n        ],\n        IntentCategory.LEARNING: [\n            r\'\\b(learn|understand|explain|teach|tutorial)\\b\',\n            r\'\\b(what is|how does|why does)\\b\',\n        ],\n        IntentCategory.CREATION: [\n            r\'\\b(design|develop|write|compose|draft)\\b\',\n            r\'\\b(document|report|proposal|plan|specification)\\b\',\n        ],\n        IntentCategory.ANALYSIS: [\n            r\'\\b(analyze|evaluate|assess|review|examine)\\b\',\n            r\'\\b(compare|contrast|measure|calculate)\\b\',\n        ],\n        IntentCategory.TROUBLESHOOTING: [\n            r\'\\b(fix|solve|debug|error|problem|issue|broken)\\b\',\n            r\'\\b(not working|failed|wrong)\\b\',\n        ],\n        IntentCategory.EXPLORATION: [\n            r\'\\b(explore|discover|investigate|browse)\\b\',\n            r\'\\b(options|possibilities|alternatives)\\b\',\n        ],\n    }\n    \n    # Entity extraction patterns\n    ENTITY_PATTERNS = {\n        \'domain\': r\'\\b(business|engineering|financial|legal|operations|marketing|hr|sales|product)\\b\',\n        \'artifact_type\': async def classify_intent(self, user_input: str, context: Dict = None) -> Intent:\n        """\n        Classify user intent using hybrid approach:\n        1. Rule-based pattern matching\n        2. LLM-based classification (if available)\n        3. Context-aware refinement\n        """\n        context = context or {}\n        \n        # Step 1: Rule-based classification\n        rule_based_intent = self._rule_based_classification(user_input)\n        \n        # Step 2: LLM-based classification (if available)\n        if self.llm_client:\n            llm_intent = await self._llm_based_classification(user_input, context)\n            # Combine rule-based and LLM results\n            final_intent = self._combine_classifications(rule_based_intent, llm_intent)\n        else:\n            final_intent = rule_based_intent\n        \n        # Step 3: Extract entities\n        entities = self._extract_entities(user_input)\n        final_intent.entities = entities\n        \n        # Step 4: Add context\n        final_intent.context = context\n        \n        # Store in history\n        self.classification_history.append(final_intent)\n        \n        return final_intent\n    \n    def _rule_based_classification(self, user_input: str) -> Intent:\n        """Classify intent using pattern matching"""\n        user_input_lower = user_input.lower()\n        \n        # Score each intent category\n        scores = {}\n        matched_keywords = {}\n        \n        for category, patterns in self.INTENT_PATTERNS.items():\n            score = 0\n            keywords = []\n            for pattern in patterns:\n                matches = re.findall(pattern, user_input_lower)\n                if matches:\n                    score += len(matches)\n                    keywords.extend(matches)\n            scores[category] = score\n            matched_keywords[category] = keywords\n        \n        # Get highest scoring category\n        if max(scores.values()) == 0:\n            # No patterns matched, default to QUERY\n            category = IntentCategory.QUERY\n            confidence = 0.3\n            keywords = []\n        else:\n            category = max(scores, key=scores.get)\n            total_matches = sum(scores.values())\n            confidence = min(scores[category] / total_matches, 1.0) if total_matches > 0 else 0.5\n            keywords = matched_keywords[category]\n        \n        return Intent(\n            category=category,\n            confidence=confidence,\n            keywords=keywords,\n            entities={},\n            suggested_commands=[]\n        )\n    \n    async def _llm_based_classification(self, user_input: str, context: Dict) -> Intent:\n        """Classify intent using LLM"""\n        prompt = f"""Classify the user\'s intent from the following input:\n\nUser Input: "{user_input}"\n\nContext: {json.dumps(context, indent=2)}\n\nClassify into one of these categories:\n- QUERY: User wants information\n- ACTION: User wants to execute something\n- GUIDANCE: User needs help deciding\n- LEARNING: User wants to understand\n- CREATION: User wants to create something\n- ANALYSIS: User wants analysis/insights\n- TROUBLESHOOTING: User has a problem\n- EXPLORATION: User wants to explore options\n\nRespond in JSON format:\n{{\n    "category": "CATEGORY_NAME",\n    "confidence": 0.85,\n    "keywords": ["keyword1", "keyword2"],\n    "reasoning": "Brief explanation"\n}}"""\n\n        try:\n            response = await self.llm_client.generate(prompt, temperature=0.3)\n            result = json.loads(response)\n            \n            return Intent(\n                category=IntentCategory[result[\'category\']],\n                confidence=result[\'confidence\'],\n                keywords=result[\'keywords\'],\n                entities={},\n                suggested_commands=[]\n            )\n        except Exception as e:\n            # Fallback to rule-based if LLM fails\n            return self._rule_based_classification(user_input)\n    \n    def _combine_classifications(self, rule_based: Intent, llm_based: Intent) -> Intent:\n        """Combine rule-based and LLM classifications"""\n        # Weight: 40% rule-based, 60% LLM\n        if rule_based.category == llm_based.category:\n            # Agreement - high confidence\n            combined_confidence = (rule_based.confidence * 0.4 + llm_based.confidence * 0.6) * 1.2\n            combined_confidence = min(combined_confidence, 1.0)\n            category = rule_based.category\n        else:\n            # Disagreement - use LLM but lower confidence\n            combined_confidence = llm_based.confidence * 0.7\n            category = llm_based.category\n        \n        # Combine keywords\n        combined_keywords = list(set(rule_based.keywords + llm_based.keywords))\n        \n        return Intent(\n            category=category,\n            confidence=combined_confidence,\n            keywords=combined_keywords,\n            entities={},\n            suggested_commands=[]\n        )\n    \n    def _extract_entities(self, user_input: str) -> Dict[str, str]:\n        """Extract entities from user input"""\n        entities = {}\n        user_input_lower = user_input.lower()\n        \n        for entity_type, pattern in self.ENTITY_PATTERNS.items():\n            matches = re.findall(pattern, user_input_lower)\n            if matches:\n                entities[entity_type] = matches[0]  # Take first match\n        \n        return entities\n\n\nclass CapabilityMapper:\n    """Maps intents to system capabilities"""\n    \n    # Command mappings for each intent category\n    INTENT_TO_COMMANDS = {\n        IntentCategory.QUERY: {\n            \'general\': [\'/status\',       IntentCategory.LEARNING: {\n            \'system\': [\'/help\', \'/librarian overview\'],\n            \'component\': [\'/help <component>\'],\n            \'transcripts\': [\'/librarian \'constraint\': [\'/constraint add <type>\'],\n        },\n        IntentCategory.ANALYSIS: {\n            \'domain\': [\'/domain analyze\'],\n            \'impact\': [\'/domain impact\'],\n }\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.mapping_history = []\n    \n    def map_to_commands(self, intent: Intent) -> List[str]:\n        """Convert intent to executable commands"""\n        commands = []\n        \n        # Get commands for intent category\n        category_commands = self.INTENT_TO_COMMANDS.get(intent.category, {})\n        \n        # Match based on entities\n        if intent.entities:\n            for entity_type, entity_value in intent.entities.items():\n                if entity_value in category_commands:\n                    commands.extend(category_commands[entity_value])\n        \n        # Add general commands if no specific match\n        if not commands and \'general\' in category_commands:\n            commands.extend(category_commands[\'general\'])\n        \n        # Remove duplicates while preserving order\n        seen = set()\n        unique_commands = []\n        for cmd in commands:\n            if cmd not in seen:\n                seen.add(cmd)\n                unique_commands.append(cmd)\n        \n        return unique_commands\n    \n    def suggest_workflow(self, intent: Intent) -> user_input: str, context: Dict = None) -> LibrarianResponse:\n        """\n        Main entry point for Librarian interaction\n        \n        Args:\n            user_input: User\'s question or Search commands\n        for cmd, desc in self.knowledge_base[\'commands\'].items():\n            if query_lower in cmd.lower() or query_lower in desc.lower():\n                results.append({\n                    \'type\': \'command\',\n                    \'name\': cmd,\n                    \'description\': desc,\n                    \'relevance\': 0.9\n                })\n        \n        # Search concepts\n        for concept, desc in self.knowledge_base[\'concepts\'].items():\n            if query_lower in concept.lower() or query_lower in desc.lower():\n                results.append({\n                    \'type\': \'concept\',\n                    \'name\': concept,\n                    \'description\': desc,\n                    \'relevance\': 0.8\n                })\n        \n        # Sort by relevance\n        results.sort(key=lambda x: x[\'relevance\'], reverse=True)\n        \n        return results\n    \n    def get_transcripts(self, limit: int = 10) -> List[Dict]:\n        """Get recent conversation transcripts"""\n        return self.conversation_history[-limit:]\n    \n    def get_overview(self) -> Dict:\n        """Get system overview"""\n        return {\n            \'total_interactions\': len(self.conversation_history),\n            \'intent_distribution\': self._get_intent_distribution(),\n            \'most_common_commands\': self._get_common_commands(),\n            \'knowledge_base_size\': {\n                \'commands\': len(self.knowledge_base[\'commands\']),\n                \'concepts\': len(self.knowledge_base[\'concepts\']),\n                \'workflows\': len(self.knowledge_base[\'workflows\']),\n            }\n        }\n    \n    def _get_intent_distribution(self) -> Dict[str, int]:\n        """Get distribution of intent categories"""\n        distribution = {}\n        for entry in self.conversation_history:\n            category = entry[\'response\'].intent.category.value\n            distribution[category] = distribution.get(category, 0) + 1\n        return distribution\n    \n    def _get_common_commands(self) -> List[Tuple[str, int]]:\n        """Get most commonly suggested commands"""\n        command_counts = {}\n        for entry in self.conversation_history:\n            for cmd in entry[\'response\'].commands:\n                command_counts[cmd] = command_counts.get(cmd, 0) + 1\n        \n        # async def solidify(self, doc_id: str) -> Dict:\n        """Convert document to generative prompts"""\n        document = self.documents.get(doc_id)\n        if not document:\n            raise Version snapshot with expertise depth\n- `GenerativePrompt` - Prompt for content generation\n- `DocumentState` - 8 lifecycle states\n- `DocumentType` - 10 document categories\n\n**API Endpoints (11 new endpoints):**\n```\nPOST   /api/documents                    # Create document\nGET    /api/documents                    # List documents\nGET    /api/documents/<id>               # Get document\nPOST   /api/documents/<id>/magnify       # Magnify with domain\nPOST   /api/documents/<id>/simplify      # Simplify to essentials\nPOST   /api/documents/<id>/edit          # Apply edits\nPOST   /api/documents/<id>/solidify      # Convert to prompts\nPOST   /api/documents/<id>/template      # Save as template\nGET    /api/templates                    # List templates\nPOST   /api/templates/<id>/create        # Create from template\n```\n\n---\n\n## Test Results\n\n### All Tests Passing ✅\n\n```bash\n1. Create Document: ✅\n   - Document ID: 984eb48f-5d00-46f6-82bc-d643050e1ef7\n   - State: fuzzy\n   - Expertise depth: 0\n   - Domains: [business]\n\n2. Document State Machine\n\n**8 States:**\n```\nFuzzy → Expanding → Contracting → Template → Solidified → Generating → Generated → Archived\n```\n\n**State Transitions:**\n- **Fuzzy:** Initial general state (expertise_depth = 0)\n- **Expanding:** Adding detail via Magnify (depth increases)\n- **Contracting:** Removing detail via Simplify (depth decreases)\n- **Template:** Saved as reusable template\n- **Solidified:** Converted to generative prompts\n- **Generating:** Being generated by swarms\n- **Generated:** Final output created\n- **Archived:** Stored for reference\n\n### 2. Magnify Operation\n\n**Purpose:** Expand document with domain expertise\n\n**How it works:**\n1. Takes current document content\n2. Uses LLM to add domain-specific details\n3. Increases expertise_depth by 1\n4. Adds domain to document.domains list\n5. Creates new version with changes\n\n**LLM Prompt:**\n```\nExpand this {doc_type} with {domain} domain expertise.\nAdd detailed {domain}-specific information, considerations, and best practices.\nIncrease depth and specificity while maintaining clarity.\n```\n\n**Fallback:** Rule-based expansion if LLM fails\n\n**Example:**\n```\nInput (depth 0): "We propose a new product."\nMagnify(financial) → depth 1: Adds financial projections, ROI, budget\nMagnify(marketing) → depth 2: Adds market analysis, positioning, campaigns\n```\n\n### 3. Simplify Operation\n\n**Purpose:** Distill document to essentials\n\n**How it works:**\n1. Takes current document content\n2. Uses LLM to remove unnecessary details\n3. Decreases expertise_depth by 1 (minimum 0)\n4. Maintains core message\n5. Creates new version with changes\n\n**LLM Prompt:**\n```\nSimplify this {doc_type} to its essential points.\nRemove unnecessary details, consolidate information, focus on core concepts.\nMaintain key message while reducing complexity.\n```\n\n**Fallback:** Rule-based simplification if LLM fails\n\n**Example:**\n```\nInput (depth 2): Detailed document with financial and marketing sections\nSimplify → depth 1: Removes detailed subsections, keeps main points\nSimplify → depth 0: Core message only\n```\n\n### 4. Edit Operation\n\n**Purpose:** Apply user modifications\n\n**How it works:**\n1. User provides new content\n2. System creates new version\n3. Maintains current expertise_depth\n4. Tracks modification as \'user\' change\n5. Preserves version history\n\n**Use cases:**\n- Fix typos or errors\n- Add custom sections\n- Reorganize content\n- Update information\n\n### 5. Solidify Operation\n\n**Purpose:** Convert document to generative prompts\n\n**How it works:**\n1. Analyzes document content\n2. Uses LLM to create specific prompts\n3. Determines best swarm type for each section\n4. Estimates token requirements\n5. Creates GenerativePrompt objects\n6. Changes state to SOLIDIFIED\n\n**LLM Prompt:**\n```\nConvert this {doc_type} into generative prompts for content creation.\nCreate specific, actionable prompts for each section.\nDetermine best swarm type (CREATIVE, ANALYTICAL, HYBRID).\n```\n\n**Output:**\n- List of GenerativePrompt objects\n- Each with: prompt_text, swarm_type, estimated_tokens\n- Ready for swarm execution\n\n**Example:**\n```\nDocument: Business Proposal\nSolidified into:\n  - Prompt 1: "Generate executive summary..." (ANALYTICAL, 500 tokens)\n  - Prompt 2: "Create market analysis..." (ANALYTICAL, 800 tokens)\n  - Prompt 3: "Design marketing strategy..." (CREATIVE, 600 tokens)\n```\n\n### 6. Template System\n\n**Save as Template:**\n- Captures current document state\n- Creates reusable template\n- Stores in templates collection\n- Tags with \'template\'\n\n**Create from Template:**\n- Starts new document from template\n- Inherits structure and domains\n- Resets to FUZZY state\n- Ready for customization\n\n**Use cases:**\n- Standard document formats\n- Recurring document types\n- Best practice templates\n- Organizational standards\n\n### 7. Version Control\n\n**Complete History:**\n- Every operation creates new version\n- Tracks: content, state, depth, domains, timestamp\n- Records who modified (system or user)\n- Includes change summary\n\n**Version Metadata:**\n- Version number (incremental)\n- State at that version\n- Expertise depth\n- Domains included\n- Modification timestamp\n- Changes summary\n- Custom metadata\n\n**Benefits:**\n- Full audit trail\n- Rollback capability\n- Compare versions\n- Track evolution\n\n---\n\n## Document Types Supported\n\n**10 Types:**\n1. **Proposal** - Business proposals\n2. **Specification** - Technical specifications\n3. **Report** - Analysis reports\n4. **Plan** - Project plans\n5. **Design** - Design documents\n6. **Contract** - Legal contracts\n7. **Presentation** - Slide decks\n8. **Documentation** - Technical docs\n9. **Analysis** - Data analysis\n10. **Custom** - Any other type\n\n---\n\n## Integration with Murphy System\n\n### Workflow Integration\n\n**Document Creation Flow:**\n```\n1. User creates fuzzy document\n2. Librarian suggests domains to add\n3. Magnify with relevant domains\n4. Review and edit as needed\n5. Simplify if too detailed\n6. Solidify when ready\n7. Generate via swarms\n8. Review generated output\n9. Iterate or finalize\n```\n\n**Plan Review Integration:**\n```\nDocument → Solidify → Generates Plan\nPlan → Magnify/Simplify → Updates Document\nDocument ↔ Plan (bidirectional sync)\n```\n\n**Swarm Execution:**\n```\nSolidified Document → Generative Prompts\nPrompts → Swarm Tasks\nSwarms → Generate Content\nContent → Artifacts\n```\n\n---\n\n## API Examples\n\n### Create Document\n```bash\nPOST */\n    createPanel() {\n        const panelHTML = `\n            <div id="document-editor-panel" class="system-panel" style="display: none;">\n                <div class="panel-header">\n                    <h2>📄 Living Document Editor</h2>\n                    <button class="close-btn" onclick="documentEditorPanel.close()">×</button>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div                         <button class="control-btn" onclick="documentEditorPanel.showVersionHistory()">\n                                    📜 History\n                                </button>\n                                <button class="control-btn" onclick="documentEditorPanel.showTemplates()">\n                                    📋 Templates\n                                </button>\n                            </div>\n                        </div>\n                        <div id="document-content" class="document-content" contenteditable="false">\n                            <!--                     <button class="action-btn edit-btn" onclick="documentEditorPanel.toggleEdit()">\n                            ✏️ Edit\n                        </button>\n                        <button class="action-btn solidify-btn" onclick="documentEditorPanel.solidify()">\n                            🔒 Solidify\n                        </button>\n                        <button                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <!-- Magnify Dialog -->\n            <div id="doc-magnify-dialog" class="modal-dialog" style="display: none;">\n                <div                     <option value="financial">Financial</option>\n                        <option value="legal">Legal</option>\n                        <option value="operations">Operations</option>\n                        <option value="marketing">Marketing</option>\n                        <option value="hr">HR</option>\n                        <option value="sales">Sales</option>\n                        <option value="product">Product</option>\n                    </select>\n                    <div class="dialog-actions">\n                        <button class="btn-primary" onclick="documentEditorPanel.magnify()">Magnify</button>\n                        <button class="btn-secondary" onclick="documentEditorPanel.closeMagnifyDialog()">Cancel</button>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <!-- Save Template Dialog -->\n            <div id="save-template-dialog" class="modal-dialog" style="display: none;">\n                <div class="dialog-content">\n                    <h3>Save as Template</h3>\n                    <p>Enter a name for this template:</p>\n                    <input type="text" id="template-name-input" class="template-name-input" placeholder="Template name...">\n                    <div class="dialog-actions">\n                        <button class="btn-primary" onclick="documentEditorPanel.saveAsTemplate()">Save</button>\n                        <button class="btn-secondary" onclick="documentEditorPanel.closeSaveTemplateDialog()">Cancel</button>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <!-- Templates Dialog -->\n            <div id="templates-dialog" class="modal-dialog" style="display: none;">\n                <div class="dialog-content large">\n                    <h3>Document Templates</h3>\n                    <div id="templates-list" class="templates-list">\n                        <!-- Templates will id="doc-version-history-list" class="version-list">\n                        <!-- Version history will be listed here -->\n                    </div>\n                    <div class="dialog-actions">\n                        <button class="btn-secondary" onclick="documentEditorPanel.closeVersionHistory()">Close</button>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <!-- Prompts Dialog -->\n            <div id="prompts-dialog" class="modal-dialog" style="display: none;">\n                <div class="dialog-content large">\n                    <h3>Generative Prompts</h3>\n                    <p>Document has been solidified into the following prompts:</p>\n                    <div id="prompts-list" class="prompts-list">\n                        <!-- Prompts will be listed here -->\n                    </div>\n                    <div class="dialog-actions">\n                        <button class="btn-primary"        </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        `;\n        \n        document.body.insertAdjacentHTML(\'beforeend\', panelHTML);\n        this.addStyles();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Add CSS styles for Document Editor panel\n     */\n    addStyles() {\n        const styles = `\n            <style>\n                .document-info {\n                    background: #0a0a0a;\n           .depth-indicator {\n                    display: flex;\n                    align-items: center;\n                    gap: 10px;\n                    flex: 1;\n                }\n                \n                .depth-bar {\n                    flex: 1;\n                    height: 20px;\n                    background: #1a1a1a;\n                    border: 1px solid #333;\n padding: 3px 10px;\n                    background: #2a2a2a;\n                    border: 1px solid #00ff88;\n                    border-radius: 12px;\n                    font-size: 11px;\n      border-radius: 4px;\n                    margin-bottom: 15px;\n                }\n                \n                .editor-header {\n                    display: flex;\n                    justify-content: space-between;\n                    align-items: center;\n                    padding: 10px 15px;\n                    border-bottom: 1px solid #333;\n                }\n                \n                .editor-header h3 {\n                    margin: 0;\n                    font-size: 14px;\n                    color: #00ff88;\n                }\n                \n                .editor-controls {\n                    display: flex;\n                    gap: 8px;\n                }\n                \n                .document-content {\n                    padding: 15px;\n                    min-height: 300px;\n                    max-height: 400px;\n                    overflow-y: auto;\n                    color: #fff;\n                    line-height: 1.6;\n                    white-space: pre-wrap;\n                    font-family: \'Georgia\', serif;\n                    font-size: 14px;\n                }\n                \n                .document-content[contenteditable="true"] {\n                    border: 2px solid #00ff88;\n                    background: #0f0f0f;\n                }\n                \n                .document-actions {\n                    display: flex;\n                    gap: 10px;\n                    flex-wrap: wrap;\n                }\n                \n                .template-btn {\n                    background: #cc00cc;\n                    color: #fff;\n                }\n                \n                .template-btn:hover {\n                    background: #aa00aa;\n                }\n                \n                .template-name-input {\n                    width: 100%;\n                    padding: 10px;\n                    background: #0a0a0a;\n                    border: 1px solid #333;\n                    border-radius: 4px;\n                    color: #fff;\n                    font-size: 14px;\n                    margin-bottom: 15px;\n                }\n                \n                .templates-list {\n                    max-height: 400px;\n                    overflow-y: auto;\n                }\n                \n                .template-item {\n                    padding: 15px;\n                    margin-bottom: 10px;\n                    background: #0a0a0a;\n                    border: 1px solid #333;\n                    border-radius: 4px;\n                    cursor: pointer;\n                    transition: all 0.2s;\n                }\n                \n                .template-item:hover {\n                    border-color: #00ff88;\n                    background: #1a1a1a;\n                }\n                \n                .template-name {\n                    font-weight: 600;\n                    color: #00ff88;\n                    margin-bottom: 5px;\n                }\n                \n                .template-type {\n                    color: #666;\n                    font-size: 12px;\n                }\n                \n                .prompts-list {\n                    max-height: 400px;\n                    overflow-y: auto;\n                }\n                \n                .prompt-item {\n                    padding: 15px;\n                    margin-bottom: 10px;\n                    background: #0a0a0a;\n                    border-left: 3px solid #00ff88;\n                    border-radius: 4px;\n                }\n                \n                .prompt-swarm-type {\n                    display: inline-block;\n                    padding: 3px 10px;\n                    background: #2a2a2a;\n                    border-radius: 12px;\n                    font-size: 11px;\n                    font-weight: 600;\n                    color: #00ff88;\n                    margin-bottom: 8px;\n                }\n                \n                .prompt-text {\n                    color: #ccc;\n                    font-size: 13px;\n                    line-height: 1.5;\n                }\n                \n                .prompt-tokens {\n                    color: #666;\n                    font-size: 11px;\n                    margin-top: 5px;\n                }\n            </style>\n        `;\n        \n        document.head.insertAdjacentHTML(\'beforeend\', styles);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Attach event listeners\n     */\n    attachEventListeners() {\n        // Close on Escape key\n        document.addEventListener(\'keydown\', (e) => {\n            if (e.key === \'Escape\') {\n                if (this.isEditing) {\n                    this.cancelEdit();\n                } else {\n                    this.close();\n                }\n                this.closeMagnifyDialog();\n                this.closeSaveTemplateDialog();\n                this.closeTemplates();\n                this.closeVersionHistory();\n                this.closePrompts();\n            }\n        });\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Open panel with a document\n     */\n    async open(docId) {\n        try {\n            const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/api/documents/${docId}`);\n            const data = await response.json();\n            \n            if (data.document) {\n                this.currentDocument = data.document;\n                this.displayDocument();\n                document.getElementById(\'document-editor-panel\').style.display = \'flex\';\n            }\n        } catch (error) {\n            console.error(\'Error loading document:\', error);\n            alert(\'Failed to load document\');\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create new document\n     */\n    async createNew(docType = \'custom\', name = \'New Document\') {\n        try {\n            const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/api/documents`, {\n                method: \'POST\',\n                headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n                body: JSON.stringify({\n                    name: name,\n                    doc_type: docType,\n                    description: `New ${docType} document`,\n                    content: \'Start writing your document here...\',\n                    domains: [],\n                    tags: []\n                })\n            });\n            \n            const data = await response.json();\n            \n            if (data.success) {\n                this.currentDocument = data.document;\n                this.displayDocument();\n                document.getElementById(\'document-editor-panel\').style.display = \'flex\';\n                this.toggleEdit(); // Start in edit mode\n            }\n        } catch (error) {\n            console.error(\'Error creating document:\', error);\n            alert(\'Failed to create document\');\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Display document in the panel\n     */\n    displayDocument() {\n        if (!this.currentDocument) return;\n        \n        // Update document info\n        document.getElementById(\'doc-name\').textContent = this.currentDocument.name;\n        document.getElementById(\'doc-type\').textContent = this.currentDocument.doc_type;\n        \n        const stateBadge = document.getElementById(\'doc-state\');\n        stateBadge.textContent = this.currentDocument.current_state;\n        stateBadge.className = `state-badge state-${this.currentDocument.current_state}`;\n        \n        // Update depth indicator\n        const depth = this.currentDocument.expertise_depth;\n        const maxDepth = 5; // Assume max depth of 5\n        const percentage = Math.min((depth / maxDepth) * 100, 100);\n        \n        const depthBar = document.getElementById(\'depth-bar\');\n        depthBar.style.setProperty(\'--depth-percentage\', `${percentage}%`);\n        depthBar.style.width = `${percentage}%`;\n        \n        document.getElementById(\'depth-value\').textContent = depth;\n        \n        // Update domain tags\n        const domainsDiv = document.getElementById(\'doc-domains\');\n        domainsDiv.innerHTML = \'\';\n        \n        if (this.currentDocument.domains.length === 0) {\n            domainsDiv.innerHTML = \'<span style="color: #666;">No domains</span>\';\n        } else {\n            this.currentDocument.domains.forEach(domain => {\n                const tag = document.createElement(\'span\');\n                tag.className = \'domain-tag\';\n                tag.textContent = domain;\n                domainsDiv.appendChild(tag);\n            });\n        }\n        \n        // Display current version content\n        const currentVersion = this.currentDocument.versions[this.currentDocument.current_version - 1];\n        const contentDiv = document.getElementById(\'document-content\');\n        contentDiv.textContent = currentVersion.content;\n        contentDiv.contentEditable = false;\n        \n        // Update edit button text\n        const editBtn = document.querySelector(\'.edit-btn\');\n        editBtn.textContent = \'✏️ Edit\';\n        this.isEditing = false;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Show magnify dialog\n     */\n    showMagnifyDialog() {\n        document.getElementById(\'doc-magnify-dialog\').style.display = \'flex\';\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Close magnify dialog\n     */\n    closeMagnifyDialog() {\n        document.getElementById(\'doc-magnify-dialog\').style.display = \'none\';\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Magnify document with domain\n     */\n    async magnify() {\n        const domain = document.getElementById(\'doc-magnify-domain-select\').value;\n        this.closeMagnifyDialog();\n        \n        if (this.isProcessing) return;\n        this.isProcessing = true;\n        \n        try {\n            const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/api/documents/${this.currentDocument.id}/magnify`, {\n                method: \'POST\',\n                headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n                body: JSON.stringify({ domain })\n            });\n            \n            const data = await response.json();\n            \n            if (data.success) {\n                this.currentDocument = data.document;\n                this.displayDocument();\n                if (window.addTerminalLog) {\n                    window.addTerminalLog(`✓ Document magnified with ${domain} domain (depth: ${this.currentDocument.expertise_depth})`, \'success\');\n                }\n            } else {\n                alert(\'Failed to magnify document: \' + data.error);\n            }\n        } catch (error) {\n            console.error(\'Magnify error:\', error);\n            alert(\'Failed to magnify document\');\n        } finally {\n            this.isProcessing = false;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Simplify document\n     */\n    async simplify() {\n        if (this.isProcessing) return;\n        this.isProcessing = true;\n        \n        try {\n            const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/api/documents/${this.currentDocument.id}/simplify`, {\n                method: \'POST\',\n                headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' }\n            });\n            \n            const data = await response.json();\n            \n            if (data.success) {\n                this.currentDocument = data.document;\n                this.displayDocument();\n                if (window.addTerminalLog) {\n                    window.addTerminalLog(`✓ Document simplified (depth: ${this.currentDocument.expertise_depth})`, \'success\');\n                }\n            } else {\n                alert(\'Failed to simplify document: \' + data.error);\n            }\n        } catch (error) {\n            console.error(\'Simplify error:\', error);\n            alert(\'Failed to simplify document\');\n        } finally {\n            this.isProcessing = false;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Toggle edit mode\n     */\n    toggleEdit() {\n        const contentDiv = document.getElementById(\'document-content\');\n        const editBtn = document.querySelector(\'.edit-btn\');\n        \n        if (this.isEditing) {\n            // Save changes\n            this.saveEdit();\n        } else {\n            // Enable editing\n            contentDiv.contentEditable = true;\n            contentDiv.focus();\n            editBtn.textContent = \'💾 Save\';\n            this.isEditing = true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Save edit\n     */\n    async saveEdit() {\n        const contentDiv = document.getElementById(\'document-content\');\n        const newContent = contentDiv.textContent;\n        \n        if (this.isProcessing) return;\n        this.isProcessing = true;\n        \n        try {\n            const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/api/documents/${this.currentDocument.id}/edit`, {\n                method: \'POST\',\n                headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n                body: JSON.stringify({\n                    content: newContent,\n                    summary: \'User modifications\'\n                })\n            });\n            \n            const data = await response.json();\n            \n            if (data.success) {\n                this.currentDocument = data.document;\n                this.displayDocument();\n                if (window.addTerminalLog) {\n                    window.addTerminalLog(\'✓ Document updated\', \'success\');\n                }\n            } else {\n                alert(\'Failed to save document: \' + data.error);\n            }\n        } catch (error) {\n            console.error(\'Save error:\', error);\n            alert(\'Failed to save document\');\n        } finally {\n            this.isProcessing = false;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Cancel edit\n     */\n    cancelEdit() {\n        this.displayDocument();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Solidify document\n     */\n    async solidify() {\n        if (this.isProcessing) return;\n        this.isProcessing = true;\n        \n        try {\n            const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/api/documents/${this.currentDocument.id}/solidify`, {\n                method: \'POST\',\n                headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' }\n            });\n            \n            const data = await response.json();\n            \n            if (data.success) {\n                this.currentDocument = data.document;\n                this.displayDocument();\n                if (window.addTerminalLog) {\n                    window.addTerminalLog(`✓ Document solidified into ${data.prompts.length} generative prompts`, \'success\');\n                }\n                // Show prompts dialog\n                this.showPrompts(data.prompts);\n            } else {\n                alert(\'Failed to solidify document: \' + data.error);\n            }\n        } catch (error) {\n            console.error(\'Solidify error:\', error);\n            alert(\'Failed to solidify document\');\n        } finally {\n            this.isProcessing = false;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Show prompts dialog\n     */\n    showPrompts(prompts) {\n        const promptsList = document.getElementById(\'prompts-list\');\n        promptsList.innerHTML = \'\';\n        \n        prompts.forEach((prompt, index) => {\n            const promptDiv = document.createElement(\'div\');\n            promptDiv.className = \'prompt-item\';\n            promptDiv.innerHTML = `\n                <span class="prompt-swarm-type">${prompt.swarm_type}</span>\n                <div class="prompt-text">${prompt.prompt_text}</div>\n                <div class="prompt-tokens">Estimated tokens: ${prompt.estimated_tokens}</div>\n            `;\n            promptsList.appendChild(promptDiv);\n        });\n        \n        document.getElementById(\'prompts-dialog\').style.display = \'flex\';\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Close prompts dialog\n     */\n    closePrompts() {\n        document.getElementById(\'prompts-dialog\').style.display = \'none\';\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Execute prompts (trigger swarm execution)\n     */\n    executePrompts() {\n        this.closePrompts();\n        if (window.addTerminalLog) {\n            window.addTerminalLog(\'🚀 Executing generative prompts via swarms...\', \'info\');\n            window.addTerminalLog(\'(Swarm execution will be implemented in Phase 4)\', \'info\');\n        }\n        // TODO: Integrate with swarm execution system in Phase 4\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Show save template dialog\n     */\n    showSaveTemplateDialog() {\n        document.getElementById(\'save-template-dialog\').style.display = \'flex\';\n        document.getElementById(\'template-name-input\').value = `${this.currentDocument.name} Template`;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Close save template dialog\n     */\n    closeSaveTemplateDialog() {\n        document.getElementById(\'save-template-dialog\').style.display = \'none\';\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Save as template\n     */\n    async saveAsTemplate() {\n        const templateName = document.getElementById(\'template-name-input\').value.trim();\n        \n        if (!templateName) {\n            alert(\'Please enter a template name\');\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        this.closeSaveTemplateDialog();\n        \n        if (this.isProcessing) return;\n        this.isProcessing = true;\n        \n        try {\n            const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/api/documents/${this.currentDocument.id}/template`, {\n                method: \'POST\',\n                headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n                body: JSON.stringify({ name: templateName })\n            });\n            \n            const data = await response.json();\n            \n            if (data.success) {\n                if (window.addTerminalLog) {\n                    window.addTerminalLog(`✓ Template \'${templateName}\' created`, \'success\');\n                }\n            } else {\n                alert(\'Failed to save template: \' + data.error);\n            }\n        } catch (error) {\n            console.error(\'Save template error:\', error);\n            alert(\'Failed to save template\');\n        } finally {\n            this.isProcessing = false;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Show templates dialog\n     */\n    async showTemplates() {\n        try {\n            const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/api/templates`);\n            const data = await response.json();\n            \n            const templatesList = document.getElementById(\'templates-list\');\n            templatesList.innerHTML = \'\';\n            \n            if (data.templates.length === 0) {\n                templatesList.innerHTML = \'<p style="color: #666; text-align: center; padding: 20px;">No templates available</p>\';\n            } else {\n                data.templates.forEach(template => {\n                    const templateDiv = document.createElement(\'div\');\n                    templateDiv.className = \'template-item\';\n                    templateDiv.onclick = () => this.createFromTemplate(template.id, template.name);\n                    templateDiv.innerHTML = `\n                        <div class="template-name">${template.name}</div>\n                        <div class="template-type">${template.doc_type}</div>\n                    `;\n                    templatesList.appendChild(templateDiv);\n                });\n            }\n            \n            document.getElementById(\'templates-dialog\').style.display = \'flex\';\n        } catch (error) {\n            console.error(\'Load templates error:\', error);\n            alert(\'Failed to load templates\');\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Close templates dialog\n     */\n    closeTemplates() {\n        document.getElementById(\'templates-dialog\').style.display = \'none\';\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create document from template\n     */\n    async createFromTemplate(templateId, templateName) {\n        this.closeTemplates();\n        \n        const docName = prompt(`Enter name for new document (from template: ${templateName}):`, `New ${templateName}`);\n        if (!docName) return;\n        \n        try {\n            const response = await fetch(`${this.apiBase}/api/templates/${templateId}/create`, {\n                method: \'POST\',\n                headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n                body: JSON.stringify({ name: docName })\n            });\n            \n            const data = await response.json();\n            \n            if (data.success) {\n                this.currentDocument = data.document;\n                this.displayDocument();\n                if (window.addTerminalLog) {\n                    window.addTerminalLog(`✓ Document \'${docName}\' created from template`, \'success\');\n                }\n            } else {\n                alert(\'Failed to create from template: \' + data.error);\n            }\n        } catch (error) {\n            console.error(\'Create from template error:\', error);\n            alert(\'Failed to create from template\');\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Show version history\n     */\n    showVersionHistory() {\n        const historyList = document.getElementById(\'doc-version-history-list\');\n        historyList.innerHTML = \'\';\n        \n        this.currentDocument.versions.forEach((version, index) => {\n            const versionDiv = document.createElement(\'div\');\n            versionDiv.className = \'version-item\';\n            versionDiv.innerHTML = `\n                <div class="version-header">\n
